posted:Posted April 19, 2023
msg:The hotel looks old and tired but the good smell at the loby shows that this is a 5 stars hotel. The check in was easy, i was given an upgrade to the newly renovated room as well as late check out. Really nice gesture from the hotel staff! Room was spacious and modern, really up to the standard for 5 stars hotel. They have international plug which was great, bath tub, complete amenities but the aircon a bit warm for me.

Location was great, 10-12 rmb taxi from luohu port, walking distance to guomao subway, short distance to nearest shopping mall, dongmen st, and last but the least you can walk to shenzen famous queen spa!

Check in staff has limited english but the guy from concierge had better english! 

All in all great stay for a first timer and solo in shenzen, will recommend to other people who look for accomodation in luohu area..

In the center of Luohu, land is at a premium, but the underground parking lot is very large. The hotel lobby smells good, and the dim lighting creates a quiet, calm and old-school a**osphere. As soon as you enter the house, there is a lacquered red wardrobe standing next to it, giving off a classic feel.

The hotel must have been open for many years, and the murals on the walls record some historical stages. The hotels opened near the Luohu Port were originally intended to entertain returning Hong Kong tourists and foreign tourists. However, times have changed. For a modern big city like Shenzhen, the development in the past few decades has been too fast. There are more and better hotels such as After two generations, they have sprung up like bamboo shoots, and each wave is stronger than the last. Physical hotels are large in size, expensive to decorate, and difficult to change. Naturally, these original luxury hotels were left behind and slowly became "old".

Although the "old" hotel is old, it has its own feelings. Those are the past worth remembering, and the familiar memories and people...are also the ones that have supported the Sunshine Hotel ten years after another.
